## 0.4 add the cli (files to copy–paste)

**create file:** `~/OneDrive/Documents/template_refactor_gpt/preview-launcher/refactor-cli/package.json`
```json
{
  "name": "refactor-cli",
  "version": "0.1.0",
  "private": true,
  "type": "commonjs",
  "bin": { "refactor": "./bin/index.js" },
  "dependencies": {
    "chalk": "^5.3.0",
    "extract-zip": "^2.0.1",
    "fs-extra": "^11.2.0",
    "globby": "^14.0.2",
    "yargs": "^17.7.2"
  }
}
```

**create file:** `~/OneDrive/Documents/template_refactor_gpt/preview-launcher/refactor-cli/bin/index.js`
```js
#!/usr/bin/env node
const path = require("path");
const fs = require("fs-extra");
const yargs = require("yargs/yargs");
const { hideBin } = require("yargs/helpers");
const chalk = require("chalk");
const extract = require("extract-zip");
const globby = require("globby");

/* ---------- helpers ---------- */
const ROOT = process.cwd();
const PREVIEW_PUBLIC = path.join(ROOT, "public", "template");
const MANIFEST = path.join(PREVIEW_PUBLIC, "manifest.json");

function ok(msg){ console.log(chalk.green("✔"), msg); }
function info(msg){ console.log(chalk.cyan("ℹ"), msg); }
function toLabel(slug){
  return slug.replace(/^px[-_]?|[-_]?html$/g,"")
             .replace(/[-_]/g," ")
             .replace(/\b\w/g, m => m.toUpperCase()).trim();
}
async function loadManifest(){
  if(!(await fs.pathExists(MANIFEST))) return { templates: [] };
  try { return JSON.parse(await fs.readFile(MANIFEST,"utf8")); }
  catch { return { templates: [] }; }
}
async function saveManifest(json){
  await fs.ensureDir(path.dirname(MANIFEST));
  await fs.writeFile(MANIFEST, JSON.stringify(json, null, 2), "utf8");
}
async function detectTemplate(dir){
  const entries = (await fs.pathExists(dir)) ? await fs.readdir(dir) : [];
  const variants = [];
  for(const name of entries){
    const vdir = path.join(dir, name);
    const st = await fs.stat(vdir).catch(()=>null);
    if(!st || !st.isDirectory()) continue;
    const htmls = await globby("*.html", { cwd: vdir });
    const hasAssets = await fs.pathExists(path.join(vdir,"assets"));
    if(htmls.length || hasAssets) variants.push({ name, pages: htmls.sort() });
  }
  if(variants.length === 0){
    const htmls = await globby("*.html", { cwd: dir });
    return { variants: [{ name: "default", pages: htmls.sort() }] };
  }
  return { variants };
}

/* ---------- ingest ---------- */
async function cmdIngest(argv){
  const { zip, slug: slugIn, variant: variantIn } = argv;
  if(!zip){ console.error("Missing --zip <path-to-zip>"); process.exit(1); }
  const slug = slugIn || path.basename(zip).replace(/\.zip$/i,"");
  const tmp = path.join(ROOT, ".tmp", slug);
  await fs.remove(tmp); await fs.ensureDir(tmp);

  info(`Extracting ZIP → ${path.relative(ROOT,tmp)}`);
  await extract(zip, { dir: tmp });

  // find actual root (some zips wrap files in a single folder)
  const kids = await fs.readdir(tmp);
  let sourceRoot = tmp;
  if(kids.length === 1){
    const p = path.join(tmp,kids[0]);
    if((await fs.stat(p)).isDirectory()) sourceRoot = p;
  }

  const targetBase = path.join(PREVIEW_PUBLIC, slug);
  await fs.ensureDir(targetBase);

  const detected = await detectTemplate(sourceRoot);
  if(variantIn){
    const target = path.join(targetBase, variantIn);
    await fs.ensureDir(target);
    await fs.copy(sourceRoot, target, { overwrite: true });
    ok(`Copied → ${path.relative(ROOT,target)}`);
  } else {
    for(const v of detected.variants){
      const src = v.name === "default" ? sourceRoot : path.join(sourceRoot, v.name);
      const target = path.join(targetBase, v.name);
      await fs.ensureDir(target);
      await fs.copy(src, target, { overwrite: true });
      ok(`Variant ${v.name} → ${path.relative(ROOT,target)}`);
    }
  }

  const manifest = await loadManifest();
  const label = toLabel(slug);
  const fresh = await detectTemplate(targetBase);
  const pages = Array.from(new Set(fresh.variants.flatMap(v=>v.pages))).sort();
  const variants = fresh.variants.map(v=>v.name).sort();

  const entry = { slug, label, variants, pages: pages.length ? pages : ["index.html"] };
  const idx = manifest.templates.findIndex(t => t.slug === slug);
  if(idx >= 0) manifest.templates[idx] = entry; else manifest.templates.push(entry);
  await saveManifest(manifest);
  ok(`Manifest updated: ${path.relative(ROOT, MANIFEST)}`);
  ok("Ingest complete.");
}

/* ---------- generate ---------- */
async function cmdGenerate(argv){
  const { slug, variant = "default", out } = argv;
  if(!slug || !out){
    console.error("Usage: generate --slug <template-slug> --variant <name> --out kits/pex-<name>");
    process.exit(1);
  }
  const srcVariantDir = path.join(PREVIEW_PUBLIC, slug, variant);
  if(!(await fs.pathExists(srcVariantDir))){
    console.error(`Variant not found at ${path.relative(ROOT,srcVariantDir)}. Run 'ingest' first or check variant.`);
    process.exit(1);
  }

  const kitRoot = path.join(ROOT, out);
  const client = path.join(kitRoot, "client");
  const server = path.join(kitRoot, "server");
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "public", slug, variant));
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "src", "pages"));
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "src", "lib"));
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(server, "src", "routes"));

  // copy static assets
  await fs.copy(srcVariantDir, path.join(client, "public", slug, variant), { overwrite: true });
  ok(`Static copied → ${path.relative(ROOT, path.join(client,"public",slug,variant))}`);

  // --- server scaffold ---
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(server, "package.json"), JSON.stringify({
    name: `${out.replace(/[\/\\]/g,"-")}-server`,
    version: "1.0.0", private: true, type: "module",
    scripts: { dev: "node src/index.js", start: "node src/index.js" },
    dependencies: { cors: "^2.8.5", dotenv: "^16.4.5", express: "^4.19.2", morgan: "^1.10.0" }
  }, null, 2));
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(server, ".env.example"), "PORT=5050\n");
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(server, "src", "routes", "health.js"),
`import { Router } from "express";
const router = Router();
router.get("/", (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, service: "health", timestamp: new Date().toISOString() }));
export default router;`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(server, "src", "index.js"),
`import express from "express";
import cors from "cors";
import morgan from "morgan";
import dotenv from "dotenv";
import health from "./routes/health.js";
dotenv.config();
const app = express();
app.use(cors()); app.use(morgan("dev")); app.use(express.json());
app.use("/api/health", health);
app.get("/", (_req,res) => res.json({ ok:true, service:"${out}", endpoints:["/api/health"] }));
const port = process.env.PORT || 5050;
app.listen(port, () => console.log(\`API listening on http://localhost:\${port}\`));`);

  // --- client scaffold (vite + tailwind) ---
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "package.json"), JSON.stringify({
    name: `${out.replace(/[\/\\]/g,"-")}-client`,
    version: "1.0.0", private: true, type: "module",
    scripts: { dev: "vite", build: "vite build", preview: "vite preview" },
    dependencies: { axios: "^1.7.2", react: "^18.2.0", "react-dom": "^18.2.0", "react-router-dom": "^6.26.0" },
    devDependencies: {
      "@vitejs/plugin-react": "^4.3.0", vite: "^5.4.0",
      tailwindcss: "^3.4.10", autoprefixer: "^10.4.20", postcss: "^8.4.41"
    }
  }, null, 2));
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "vite.config.js"),
`import { defineConfig } from "vite";
import react from "@vitejs/plugin-react";
export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [react()],
  server: { port: 5174, proxy: { "/api": { target: "http://localhost:5050", changeOrigin: true } } },
  preview: { port: 5174 }
});`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "index.html"),
`<!doctype html><html lang="en"><head>
<meta charset="UTF-8"/><meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1.0"/>
<title>${toLabel(slug)} — MERN Kit</title>
<link rel="icon" type="image/svg+xml" href="/favicon.svg"/>
<link rel="stylesheet" href="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/css/main.css"/>
<noscript><link rel="stylesheet" href="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/css/noscript.css"/></noscript>
</head><body>
<div id="root"></div>
<script type="module" src="/src/main.jsx"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/jquery.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/jquery.scrolly.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/jquery.scrollex.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/browser.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/breakpoints.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/util.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/main.js"></script>
</body></html>`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "tailwind.config.js"),
`export default { content:["./index.html","./src/**/*.{js,jsx,ts,tsx}"], theme:{ extend:{} }, plugins:[] };`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "postcss.config.js"),
`export default { plugins: { tailwindcss:{}, autoprefixer:{} } };`);
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client,"src"));
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client,"src","index.css"),
`@tailwind base; @tailwind components; @tailwind utilities;`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client,"src","main.jsx"),
`import React from "react";
import { createRoot } from "react-dom/client";
import { createBrowserRouter, RouterProvider } from "react-router-dom";
import App from "./App.jsx";
import Home from "./pages/Home.jsx";
import "./index.css";
const router = createBrowserRouter([{ path:"/", element:<App/>, children:[{ index:true, element:<Home/> }] }]);
createRoot(document.getElementById("root")).render(<React.StrictMode><RouterProvider router={router} future={{ v7_startTransition: true }}/></React.StrictMode>);`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client,"src","App.jsx"),
`import { Outlet, NavLink } from "react-router-dom";
export default function App(){
  return (<div className="min-h-screen">
    <nav className="px-4 py-2 border-b">
      <NavLink to="/" end className="mr-4">Home</NavLink>
    </nav>
    <Outlet/>
  </div>);
}`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client,"src","pages","Home.jsx"),
`export default function Home(){
  return (<iframe title="Home" src="/${slug}/${variant}/index.html" style={{ width:"100%", height:"calc(100vh - 56px)", border:0 }} />);
}`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client,"src","lib","api.js"),
`import axios from "axios"; export const api = axios.create({ baseURL:"/api", headers:{ "Content-Type":"application/json" } });`);
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "public"));
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "public", "favicon.svg"),
`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 64 64"><rect width="64" height="64" rx="12" fill="#0f172a"/><text x="50%" y="50%" dominant-baseline="middle" text-anchor="middle" font-family="Arial" font-size="28" fill="#60a5fa">K</text></svg>`);

  ok(`Kit generated at: ${path.relative(ROOT, kitRoot)}`);
  info(`Next:
  1) API:    cd ${path.relative(ROOT, path.join(kitRoot,"server"))} && cp .env.example .env && npm i && npm run dev
  2) Client: cd ${path.relative(ROOT, path.join(kitRoot,"client"))} && npm i && npm run dev
  3) Open http://localhost:5174`);
}

/* ---------- yargs ---------- */
yargs(hideBin(process.argv))
  .scriptName("refactor")
  .command("ingest","Ingest a template ZIP into the previewer and update manifest",(y)=>
    y.option("zip",{type:"string", demandOption:true})
     .option("slug",{type:"string"})
     .option("variant",{type:"string"})
  , (argv)=>cmdIngest(argv).catch(e=>{ console.error(e); process.exit(1); }))
  .command("generate","Generate a MERN+Tailwind kit from a template variant",(y)=>
    y.option("slug",{type:"string", demandOption:true})
     .option("variant",{type:"string", default:"default"})
     .option("out",{type:"string", demandOption:true})
  , (argv)=>cmdGenerate(argv).catch(e=>{ console.error(e); process.exit(1); }))
  .demandCommand(1).help().argv;
```

### Add a root script to call the CLI


### Create the CLI files

**Create:** `refactor-cli/package.json`
```json
{
  "name": "refactor-cli",
  "version": "0.1.0",
  "private": true,
  "type": "commonjs",
  "bin": { "refactor": "./bin/index.js" },
  "dependencies": {
    "chalk": "^5.3.0",
    "extract-zip": "^2.0.1",
    "fs-extra": "^11.2.0",
    "globby": "^14.0.2",
    "yargs": "^17.7.2"
  }
}
```

**Create:** `refactor-cli/bin/index.js`
```js
#!/usr/bin/env node
const path = require("path");
const fs = require("fs-extra");
const yargs = require("yargs/yargs");
const { hideBin } = require("yargs/helpers");
const chalk = require("chalk");
const extract = require("extract-zip");
const globby = require("globby");

const ROOT = process.cwd();
const PREVIEW_PUBLIC = path.join(ROOT, "public", "template");
const MANIFEST = path.join(PREVIEW_PUBLIC, "manifest.json");

function ok(m){ console.log(chalk.green("✔"), m); }
function info(m){ console.log(chalk.cyan("ℹ"), m); }
function toLabel(slug){
  return slug.replace(/^px[-_]?|[-_]?html$/g,"")
             .replace(/[-_]/g," ")
             .replace(/\b\w/g, m => m.toUpperCase()).trim();
}
async function loadManifest(){ try{
  return (await fs.pathExists(MANIFEST)) ? JSON.parse(await fs.readFile(MANIFEST,"utf8")) : { templates: [] };
}catch{ return { templates: [] };}}
async function saveManifest(json){
  await fs.ensureDir(path.dirname(MANIFEST));
  await fs.writeFile(MANIFEST, JSON.stringify(json, null, 2), "utf8");
}
async function detectTemplate(dir){
  const entries = (await fs.pathExists(dir)) ? await fs.readdir(dir) : [];
  const variants = [];
  for(const name of entries){
    const vdir = path.join(dir,name);
    const st = await fs.stat(vdir).catch(()=>null);
    if(!st || !st.isDirectory()) continue;
    const htmls = await globby("*.html", { cwd: vdir });
    const hasAssets = await fs.pathExists(path.join(vdir,"assets"));
    if(htmls.length || hasAssets) variants.push({ name, pages: htmls.sort() });
  }
  if(variants.length === 0){
    const htmls = await globby("*.html", { cwd: dir });
    return { variants: [{ name: "default", pages: htmls.sort() }] };
  }
  return { variants };
}

/* ingest */
async function cmdIngest(argv){
  const { zip, slug: slugIn, variant: variantIn } = argv;
  if(!zip){ console.error("Missing --zip <path-to-zip>"); process.exit(1); }
  const slug = slugIn || path.basename(zip).replace(/\.zip$/i,"");
  const tmp = path.join(ROOT, ".tmp", slug);
  await fs.remove(tmp); await fs.ensureDir(tmp);

  info(`Extracting ZIP → ${path.relative(ROOT,tmp)}`);
  await extract(zip, { dir: tmp });

  const kids = await fs.readdir(tmp);
  let sourceRoot = tmp;
  if(kids.length === 1){
    const p = path.join(tmp,kids[0]);
    if((await fs.stat(p)).isDirectory()) sourceRoot = p;
  }

  const targetBase = path.join(PREVIEW_PUBLIC, slug);
  await fs.ensureDir(targetBase);

  const detected = await detectTemplate(sourceRoot);
  if(variantIn){
    const target = path.join(targetBase, variantIn);
    await fs.ensureDir(target);
    await fs.copy(sourceRoot, target, { overwrite: true });
    ok(`Copied → ${path.relative(ROOT,target)}`);
  } else {
    for(const v of detected.variants){
      const src = v.name === "default" ? sourceRoot : path.join(sourceRoot, v.name);
      const target = path.join(targetBase, v.name);
      await fs.ensureDir(target);
      await fs.copy(src, target, { overwrite: true });
      ok(`Variant ${v.name} → ${path.relative(ROOT,target)}`);
    }
  }

  const manifest = await loadManifest();
  const label = toLabel(slug);
  const fresh = await detectTemplate(targetBase);
  const pages = Array.from(new Set(fresh.variants.flatMap(v=>v.pages))).sort();
  const variants = fresh.variants.map(v=>v.name).sort();

  const entry = { slug, label, variants, pages: pages.length ? pages : ["index.html"] };
  const i = manifest.templates.findIndex(t => t.slug === slug);
  if(i >= 0) manifest.templates[i] = entry; else manifest.templates.push(entry);
  await saveManifest(manifest);
  ok(`Manifest updated: ${path.relative(ROOT, MANIFEST)}`);
  ok("Ingest complete.");
}

/* generate */
async function cmdGenerate(argv){
  const { slug, variant = "default", out } = argv;
  if(!slug || !out){
    console.error("Usage: generate --slug <template-slug> --variant <name> --out kits/pex-<name>");
    process.exit(1);
  }
  const srcVariantDir = path.join(PREVIEW_PUBLIC, slug, variant);
  if(!(await fs.pathExists(srcVariantDir))){
    console.error(`Variant not found at ${path.relative(ROOT,srcVariantDir)}. Run 'ingest' first or check variant.`);
    process.exit(1);
  }

  const kitRoot = path.join(ROOT, out);
  const client = path.join(kitRoot, "client");
  const server = path.join(kitRoot, "server");
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "public", slug, variant));
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "src", "pages"));
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "src", "lib"));
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(server, "src", "routes"));

  await fs.copy(srcVariantDir, path.join(client, "public", slug, variant), { overwrite: true });
  ok(`Static copied → ${path.relative(ROOT, path.join(client,"public",slug,variant))}`);

  await fs.writeFile(path.join(server, "package.json"), JSON.stringify({
    name: `${out.replace(/[\/\\]/g,"-")}-server`,
    version: "1.0.0", private: true, type: "module",
    scripts: { dev: "node src/index.js", start: "node src/index.js" },
    dependencies: { cors: "^2.8.5", dotenv: "^16.4.5", express: "^4.19.2", morgan: "^1.10.0" }
  }, null, 2));
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(server, ".env.example"), "PORT=5050\n");
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(server, "src", "routes", "health.js"),
`import { Router } from "express";
const router = Router();
router.get("/", (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, service: "health", timestamp: new Date().toISOString() }));
export default router;`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(server, "src", "index.js"),
`import express from "express";
import cors from "cors";
import morgan from "morgan";
import dotenv from "dotenv";
import health from "./routes/health.js";
dotenv.config();
const app = express();
app.use(cors()); app.use(morgan("dev")); app.use(express.json());
app.use("/api/health", health);
app.get("/", (_req,res) => res.json({ ok:true, service:"${out}", endpoints:["/api/health"] }));
const port = process.env.PORT || 5050;
app.listen(port, () => console.log(\`API listening on http://localhost:\${port}\`));`);

  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "package.json"), JSON.stringify({
    name: `${out.replace(/[\/\\]/g,"-")}-client`,
    version: "1.0.0", private: true, type: "module",
    scripts: { dev: "vite", build: "vite build", preview: "vite preview" },
    dependencies: { axios: "^1.7.2", react: "^18.2.0", "react-dom": "^18.2.0", "react-router-dom": "^6.26.0" },
    devDependencies: {
      "@vitejs/plugin-react": "^4.3.0", vite: "^5.4.0",
      tailwindcss: "^3.4.10", autoprefixer: "^10.4.20", postcss: "^8.4.41"
    }
  }, null, 2));
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "vite.config.js"),
`import { defineConfig } from "vite";
import react from "@vitejs/plugin-react";
export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [react()],
  server: { port: 5174, proxy: { "/api": { target: "http://localhost:5050", changeOrigin: true } } },
  preview: { port: 5174 }
});`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "index.html"),
`<!doctype html><html lang="en"><head>
<meta charset="UTF-8"/><meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1.0"/>
<title>${toLabel(slug)} — MERN Kit</title>
<link rel="icon" type="image/svg+xml" href="/favicon.svg"/>
<link rel="stylesheet" href="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/css/main.css"/>
<noscript><link rel="stylesheet" href="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/css/noscript.css"/></noscript>
</head><body>
<div id="root"></div>
<script type="module" src="/src/main.jsx"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/jquery.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/jquery.scrolly.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/jquery.scrollex.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/browser.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/breakpoints.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/util.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/main.js"></script>
</body></html>`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "tailwind.config.js"),
`export default { content:["./index.html","./src/**/*.{js,jsx,ts,tsx}"], theme:{ extend:{} }, plugins:[] };`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "postcss.config.js"),
`export default { plugins: { tailwindcss:{}, autoprefixer:{} } };`);
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client,"src"));
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client,"src","index.css"),
`@tailwind base; @tailwind components; @tailwind utilities;`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client,"src","main.jsx"),
`import React from "react";
import { createRoot } from "react-dom/client";
import { createBrowserRouter, RouterProvider } from "react-router-dom";
import App from "./App.jsx";
import Home from "./pages/Home.jsx";
import "./index.css";
const router = createBrowserRouter([{ path:"/", element:<App/>, children:[{ index:true, element:<Home/> }] }]);
createRoot(document.getElementById("root")).render(<React.StrictMode><RouterProvider router={router} future={{ v7_startTransition: true }}/></React.StrictMode>);`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client,"src","App.jsx"),
`import { Outlet, NavLink } from "react-router-dom";
export default function App(){
  return (<div className="min-h-screen">
    <nav className="px-4 py-2 border-b">
      <NavLink to="/" end className="mr-4">Home</NavLink>
    </nav>
    <Outlet/>
  </div>);
}`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client,"src","pages","Home.jsx"),
`export default function Home(){
  return (<iframe title="Home" src="/${slug}/${variant}/index.html" style={{ width:"100%", height:"calc(100vh - 56px)", border:0 }} />);
}`);
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client,"src","lib","api.js"),
`import axios from "axios"; export const api = axios.create({ baseURL:"/api", headers:{ "Content-Type":"application/json" } });`);
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "public"));
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "public", "favicon.svg"),
`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 64 64"><rect width="64" height="64" rx="12" fill="#0f172a"/><text x="50%" y="50%" dominant-baseline="middle" text-anchor="middle" font-family="Arial" font-size="28" fill="#60a5fa">K</text></svg>`);

  ok(`Kit generated at: ${path.relative(ROOT, kitRoot)}`);
  info(`Next:
  1) API:    cd ${path.relative(ROOT, path.join(kitRoot,"server"))} && cp .env.example .env && npm i && npm run dev
  2) Client: cd ${path.relative(ROOT, path.join(kitRoot,"client"))} && npm i && npm run dev
  3) Open http://localhost:5174`);
}

/* yargs */
yargs(hideBin(process.argv))
  .scriptName("refactor")
  .command("ingest","Ingest a template ZIP into the previewer and update manifest",(y)=>
    y.option("zip",{type:"string", demandOption:true})
     .option("slug",{type:"string"})
     .option("variant",{type:"string"})
  , (argv)=>cmdIngest(argv).catch(e=>{ console.error(e); process.exit(1); }))
  .command("generate","Generate a MERN+Tailwind kit from a template variant",(y)=>
    y.option("slug",{type:"string", demandOption:true})
     .option("variant",{type:"string", default:"default"})
     .option("out",{type:"string", demandOption:true})
  , (argv)=>cmdGenerate(argv).catch(e=>{ console.error(e); process.exit(1); }))
  .demandCommand(1).help().argv;
```

**Install CLI deps:**
```bash
cd refactor-cli
npm install
cd ..
```

**Smoke test:**
```bash
npm run refactor -- --help
npm run refactor -- ingest --help
npm run refactor -- generate --help
```

ASSISTANT:
Good catch — `?? NUL` means a stray file named **`NUL`** got created in your repo root.  
That happened because we used a Windows-style redirect (`2> NUL`) in **Git Bash** earlier. In Git Bash the null device is **`/dev/null`**, so `2> NUL` created a real file instead of discarding output. My bad!

Here’s the quick fix and the next checks.

## 1) Delete the stray `NUL` file
**Folder:** `~/OneDrive/Documents/template_refactor_gpt/preview-launcher`
```bash
rm -f -- NUL
```
(If you’re in PowerShell: `Remove-Item -Force .\NUL`.)

> Tip for the future:
> - **Git Bash:** redirect to `/dev/null` → `2>/dev/null`
> - **CMD.exe:** `>NUL 2>&1`
> - **PowerShell:** `*> $null` or `2> $null`

## 2) Verify clean status
**Folder:** same as above
```bash
git status --porcelain
```

ASSISTANT:
You’ve got a **JSON syntax error** in the **root `package.json`**—most likely a missing comma right before the new `"refactor"` script.

### Why it broke
JSON requires a comma between properties. If your `"scripts"` looked like this (❌ missing comma):
```json
"scripts": {
  "dev": "vite",
  "build": "vite build",
  "preview": "vite preview"
  "refactor": "node refactor-cli/bin/index.js"
}
```
npm will throw the `EJSONPARSE` error you saw.

---

```json
"scripts": {
```

# Why this happened
- Our generator copied the folder correctly, but Elemental’s page needs **both** `dropotron` and `scrolly` **included before** `main.js`. If one is missing (or loaded after), `main.js` calls fail (e.g., `$('#nav > ul').dropotron(...)`).

## Optional hardening (no more plugin crashes)
If you’d like an extra safety net, add two defensive shims **at the very top** of:
`kits/pex-elemental/client/public/px-elemental-html/cyan/assets/js/main.js`
```js
window.jQuery = window.jQuery || window.$;
if (jQuery && !jQuery.fn.scrolly)    jQuery.fn.scrolly    = function(){ return this; };

```
This prevents crashes even if a plugin script goes missing later.

## Optional: teach the generator to stub missing plugins automatically
So the next kits won’t need manual edits if a template omits a plugin.

### 1) Patch the CLI (explain)
- After copying the variant to the kit, we’ll **check for plugin files** and, if missing, create a **safe no-op stub**.
- We’ll stub **`jquery.scrolly.min.js`** and **`jquery.dropotron.min.js`** (others can be added later).

### 2) Patch the CLI (copy–paste)

**Edit file:** `refactor-cli/bin/index.js`  
**Add this helper near the top (below other helpers):**
```js
async function ensurePluginFile(variantDir, name, content) {
  const p = path.join(variantDir, "assets", "js", name);
  if (!(await fs.pathExists(p))) {
    await fs.outputFile(p, content, "utf8");
    ok(`Stubbed ${name} (source didn’t include it).`);
  }
}
```

**Inside `cmdGenerate`**, **after** this line:
```js
await fs.copy(srcVariantDir, path.join(client, "public", slug, variant), { overwrite: true });
```
**insert:**
```js
const variantPublicDir = path.join(client, "public", slug, variant);

// Minimal, safe no-ops so pages don’t crash if the plugins are missing
await ensurePluginFile(
  variantPublicDir,
  "jquery.scrolly.min.js",
  '!function($){$.fn.scrolly=function(){return this}}(window.jQuery||window.$);'
);
await ensurePluginFile(
  variantPublicDir,
  "jquery.dropotron.min.js",
  '!function($){$.fn.dropotron=function(){return this}}(window.jQuery||window.$);'
);
```

**(Optional but helpful)**: keep the `$` shim in the generated `client/index.html` right after jQuery (we already put it there for Elemental; if you want I can fold it into the generator next).

ASSISTANT:
perfect — let’s upgrade the **generator** so it **auto-stubs missing jQuery plugins** (scrolly / scrollex / dropotron) and always injects a small **`$` shim** into the generated `client/index.html`. That way future kits render cleanly even when the original template omitted a plugin.

Below I first explain briefly, then give you full **copy-paste** code and commands (with the exact folder to run them in).

---

## What this patch does

1) After copying the selected variant into the kit, the CLI:
   - Checks for `assets/js/jquery.scrolly.min.js`
   - Checks for `assets/js/jquery.scrollex.min.js`
   - Checks for `assets/js/jquery.dropotron.min.js`
   - If any are missing, it writes a **safe no-op stub** so `main.js` won’t crash.

2) The generated `client/index.html` now includes a one-liner:
   ```html
   <script>window.$ = window.$ || window.jQuery;</script>
   ```
   right after jQuery so `$` is always defined.

---

## 1) Replace the CLI file (full copy-paste)

**Open file:** `refactor-cli/bin/index.js`  
**Replace its entire contents** with this:

```js
#!/usr/bin/env node
const path = require("path");
const fs = require("fs-extra");
const yargs = require("yargs/yargs");
const { hideBin } = require("yargs/helpers");
const chalk = require("chalk");
const extract = require("extract-zip");
const globby = require("globby");

const ROOT = process.cwd();
const PREVIEW_PUBLIC = path.join(ROOT, "public", "template");
const MANIFEST = path.join(PREVIEW_PUBLIC, "manifest.json");

function ok(m)   { console.log(chalk.green("✔"), m); }
function info(m) { console.log(chalk.cyan("ℹ"), m); }

function toLabel(slug){
  return slug
    .replace(/^px[-_]?/i, "")
    .replace(/[-_]?html$/i, "")
    .replace(/[-_]/g, " ")
    .replace(/\b\w/g, m => m.toUpperCase())
    .trim();
}

async function loadManifest(){
  try {
    if (!(await fs.pathExists(MANIFEST))) return { templates: [] };
    return JSON.parse(await fs.readFile(MANIFEST, "utf8"));
  } catch {
    return { templates: [] };
  }
}

async function saveManifest(json){
  await fs.ensureDir(path.dirname(MANIFEST));
  await fs.writeFile(MANIFEST, JSON.stringify(json, null, 2), "utf8");
}

async function detectTemplate(dir){
  const exists = await fs.pathExists(dir);
  if (!exists) return { variants: [] };

  const entries = await fs.readdir(dir);
  const variants = [];

  for (const name of entries) {
    const vdir = path.join(dir, name);
    const st = await fs.stat(vdir).catch(() => null);
    if (!st || !st.isDirectory()) continue;

    const htmls = await globby("*.html", { cwd: vdir });
    const hasAssets = await fs.pathExists(path.join(vdir, "assets"));
    if (htmls.length || hasAssets) variants.push({ name, pages: htmls.sort() });
  }

  if (variants.length === 0) {
    const htmls = await globby("*.html", { cwd: dir });
    return { variants: [{ name: "default", pages: htmls.sort() }] };
  }
  return { variants };
}

/** Ensure a plugin file exists; if not, create a tiny safe stub. */
async function ensurePluginFile(variantRoot, fileName, stubContent){
  const p = path.join(variantRoot, "assets", "js", fileName);
  if (!(await fs.pathExists(p))) {
    await fs.outputFile(p, stubContent, "utf8");
    ok(`Stubbed ${fileName} (source did not include it).`);
  }
}

/** -------- commands -------- */

async function cmdIngest(argv){
  const { zip, slug: slugIn, variant: variantIn } = argv;
  if (!zip) { console.error("Missing --zip <path-to-zip>"); process.exit(1); }

  const slug = slugIn || path.basename(zip).replace(/\.zip$/i, "");
  const tmp = path.join(ROOT, ".tmp", slug);
  await fs.remove(tmp);
  await fs.ensureDir(tmp);

  info(`Extracting ZIP → ${path.relative(ROOT, tmp)}`);
  await extract(zip, { dir: tmp });

  // if the zip has a single top-level folder, dive into it
  const kids = await fs.readdir(tmp);
  let sourceRoot = tmp;
  if (kids.length === 1) {
    const p = path.join(tmp, kids[0]);
    if ((await fs.stat(p)).isDirectory()) sourceRoot = p;
  }

  const targetBase = path.join(PREVIEW_PUBLIC, slug);
  await fs.ensureDir(targetBase);

  const detected = await detectTemplate(sourceRoot);

  if (variantIn) {
    const target = path.join(targetBase, variantIn);
    await fs.ensureDir(target);
    await fs.copy(sourceRoot, target, { overwrite: true });
    ok(`Copied → ${path.relative(ROOT, target)}`);
  } else {
    for (const v of detected.variants) {
      const src = v.name === "default" ? sourceRoot : path.join(sourceRoot, v.name);
      const target = path.join(targetBase, v.name);
      await fs.ensureDir(target);
      await fs.copy(src, target, { overwrite: true });
      ok(`Variant ${v.name} → ${path.relative(ROOT, target)}`);
    }
  }

  const manifest = await loadManifest();
  const label = toLabel(slug);
  const fresh = await detectTemplate(targetBase);
  const pages = Array.from(new Set(fresh.variants.flatMap(v => v.pages))).sort();
  const variants = fresh.variants.map(v => v.name).sort();

  const entry = { slug, label, variants, pages: pages.length ? pages : ["index.html"] };
  const i = manifest.templates.findIndex(t => t.slug === slug);
  if (i >= 0) manifest.templates[i] = entry; else manifest.templates.push(entry);

  await saveManifest(manifest);
  ok(`Manifest updated: ${path.relative(ROOT, MANIFEST)}`);
  ok("Ingest complete.");
}

async function cmdGenerate(argv){
  const { slug, variant = "default", out } = argv;
  if (!slug || !out) {
    console.error("Usage: generate --slug <template-slug> --variant <name> --out kits/pex-<name>");
    process.exit(1);
  }

  const srcVariantDir = path.join(PREVIEW_PUBLIC, slug, variant);
  if (!(await fs.pathExists(srcVariantDir))) {
    console.error(`Variant not found at ${path.relative(ROOT, srcVariantDir)}. Run 'ingest' first or check variant.`);
    process.exit(1);
  }

  const kitRoot = path.join(ROOT, out);
  const client = path.join(kitRoot, "client");
  const server = path.join(kitRoot, "server");

  // scaffold
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "public", slug, variant));
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "src", "pages"));
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "src", "lib"));
  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(server, "src", "routes"));

  // copy static
  const variantPublicDir = path.join(client, "public", slug, variant);
  await fs.copy(srcVariantDir, variantPublicDir, { overwrite: true });
  ok(`Static copied → ${path.relative(ROOT, variantPublicDir)}`);

  // --- NEW: auto-stub missing plugins so pages don't crash ---
  const pluginStubs = {
    "jquery.scrolly.min.js":   '!function($){$.fn.scrolly=function(){return this}}(window.jQuery||window.$);',
    "jquery.scrollex.min.js":  '!function($){$.fn.scrollex=function(){return this}}(window.jQuery||window.$);',
    "jquery.dropotron.min.js": '!function($){$.fn.dropotron=function(){return this}}(window.jQuery||window.$);'
  };
  for (const [file, stub] of Object.entries(pluginStubs)) {
    await ensurePluginFile(variantPublicDir, file, stub);
  }

  // server files
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(server, "package.json"), JSON.stringify({
    name: `${out.replace(/[\/\\]/g, "-")}-server`,
    version: "1.0.0",
    private: true,
    type: "module",
    scripts: { dev: "node src/index.js", start: "node src/index.js" },
    dependencies: { cors: "^2.8.5", dotenv: "^16.4.5", express: "^4.19.2", morgan: "^1.10.0" }
  }, null, 2));

  await fs.writeFile(path.join(server, ".env.example"), "PORT=5050\n");

  await fs.writeFile(path.join(server, "src", "routes", "health.js"),
`import { Router } from "express";
const router = Router();
router.get("/", (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, service: "health", timestamp: new Date().toISOString() }));
export default router;`);

  await fs.writeFile(path.join(server, "src", "index.js"),
`import express from "express";
import cors from "cors";
import morgan from "morgan";
import dotenv from "dotenv";
import health from "./routes/health.js";
dotenv.config();
const app = express();
app.use(cors());
app.use(morgan("dev"));
app.use(express.json());
app.use("/api/health", health);
app.get("/", (_req, res) => res.json({ ok: true, service: "${out}", endpoints: ["/api/health"] }));
const port = process.env.PORT || 5050;
app.listen(port, () => console.log(\`API listening on http://localhost:\${port}\`));`);

  // client files
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "package.json"), JSON.stringify({
    name: `${out.replace(/[\/\\]/g, "-")}-client`,
    version: "1.0.0",
    private: true,
    type: "module",
    scripts: { dev: "vite", build: "vite build", preview: "vite preview" },
    dependencies: {
      axios: "^1.7.2",
      react: "^18.2.0",
      "react-dom": "^18.2.0",
      "react-router-dom": "^6.26.0"
    },
    devDependencies: {
      "@vitejs/plugin-react": "^4.3.0",
      vite: "^5.4.0",
      tailwindcss: "^3.4.10",
      autoprefixer: "^10.4.20",
      postcss: "^8.4.41"
    }
  }, null, 2));

  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "vite.config.js"),
`import { defineConfig } from "vite";
import react from "@vitejs/plugin-react";
export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [react()],
  server: { port: 5174, proxy: { "/api": { target: "http://localhost:5050", changeOrigin: true } } },
  preview: { port: 5174 }
});`);

  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "index.html"),
`<!doctype html><html lang="en"><head>
<meta charset="UTF-8"/><meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width,initial-scale=1.0"/>
<title>${toLabel(slug)} — MERN Kit</title>
<link rel="icon" type="image/svg+xml" href="/favicon.svg"/>
<link rel="stylesheet" href="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/css/main.css"/>
<noscript><link rel="stylesheet" href="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/css/noscript.css"/></noscript>
</head><body>
<div id="root"></div>
<script type="module" src="/src/main.jsx"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/jquery.min.js"></script>
<script>window.$ = window.$ || window.jQuery;</script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/jquery.dropotron.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/jquery.scrolly.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/jquery.scrollex.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/browser.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/breakpoints.min.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/util.js"></script>
<script src="/${slug}/${variant}/assets/js/main.js"></script>
</body></html>`);

  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "tailwind.config.js"),
`export default { content: ["./index.html","./src/**/*.{js,jsx,ts,tsx}"], theme: { extend: {} }, plugins: [] };`);

  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "postcss.config.js"),
`export default { plugins: { tailwindcss: {}, autoprefixer: {} } };`);

  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "src"));
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "src", "index.css"), `@tailwind base; @tailwind components; @tailwind utilities;`);

  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "src", "main.jsx"),
`import React from "react";
import { createRoot } from "react-dom/client";
import { createBrowserRouter, RouterProvider } from "react-router-dom";
import App from "./App.jsx";
import Home from "./pages/Home.jsx";
import "./index.css";
const router = createBrowserRouter([{ path: "/", element: <App/>, children: [{ index: true, element: <Home/> }] }]);
createRoot(document.getElementById("root")).render(
  <React.StrictMode>
    <RouterProvider router={router} future={{ v7_startTransition: true }}/>
  </React.StrictMode>
);`);

  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "src", "App.jsx"),
`import { Outlet, NavLink } from "react-router-dom";
export default function App(){
  return (<div className="min-h-screen">
    <nav className="px-4 py-2 border-b">
      <NavLink to="/" end className="mr-4">Home</NavLink>
    </nav>
    <Outlet/>
  </div>);
}`);



  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "src", "pages"));
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "src", "pages", "Home.jsx"),
`export default function Home(){
  return (<iframe title="Home" src="/${slug}/${variant}/index.html" style={{ width:"100%", height:"calc(100vh - 56px)", border:0 }} />);
}`);

  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "src", "lib"));
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "src", "lib", "api.js"),
`import axios from "axios";
export const api = axios.create({ baseURL: "/api", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" } });`);

  await fs.ensureDir(path.join(client, "public"));
  await fs.writeFile(path.join(client, "public", "favicon.svg"),
`<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 64 64"><rect width="64" height="64" rx="12" fill="#0f172a"/><text x="50%" y="50%" dominant-baseline="middle" text-anchor="middle" font-family="Arial" font-size="28" fill="#60a5fa">K</text></svg>`);

  ok(`Kit generated at: ${path.relative(ROOT, kitRoot)}`);
  info(`Next:
  1) API:    cd ${path.relative(ROOT, path.join(kitRoot,"server"))} && cp .env.example .env && npm i && npm run dev
  2) Client: cd ${path.relative(ROOT, path.join(kitRoot,"client"))} && npm i && npm run dev
  3) Open http://localhost:5174`);
}

/** yargs wiring */
yargs(hideBin(process.argv))
  .scriptName("refactor")
  .command("ingest", "Ingest a template ZIP into the previewer and update manifest", (y) =>
    y.option("zip", { type: "string", demandOption: true })
     .option("slug", { type: "string" })
     .option("variant", { type: "string" })
  , (argv) => cmdIngest(argv).catch(e => { console.error(e); process.exit(1); }))
  .command("generate", "Generate a MERN+Tailwind kit from a template variant", (y) =>
    y.option("slug", { type: "string", demandOption: true })
     .option("variant", { type: "string", default: "default" })
     .option("out", { type: "string", demandOption: true })
  , (argv) => cmdGenerate(argv).catch(e => { console.error(e); process.exit(1); }))
  .demandCommand(1).help().argv;
```

## Quick recap of what’s now automatic
- When you `generate` a kit, the CLI:
  - Copies the chosen variant.
  - Auto-stubs missing `jquery.scrolly.min.js`, `jquery.scrollex.min.js`, `jquery.dropotron.min.js`.
  - Injects a `$` shim so `$` always maps to `jQuery`.
- Result: static templates load reliably in the kit without manual fixes.

ASSISTANT:
awesome—here’s a clear rundown of the four paths, what each does, why it matters, and where it fits in the flow. I’ll end with my recommended order so you can pick confidently.

---

# 1) Playwright visual-drift tests for each kit
**What:** Add Playwright to a kit so it launches the built client, grabs screenshots of key pages (e.g., `index.html`, `landing.html`), and compares them to a saved **baseline**. If anything changes (CSS regressions, missing assets), the test fails and shows diffs.

**Why:** Static templates are pixel-sensitive. Visual tests catch “oops” breaks early—especially helpful once we start refactoring to React + Tailwind or upgrading vendor scripts.

**What we’d add (per kit):**
- `playwright.config.ts` (points to the **built** site via `vite preview` for deterministic results)
- `tests/visual.spec.ts` (navigates to pages inside the iframe and snapshots)
- npm scripts: `test:e2e`, `test:update`
- GitHub Actions job to run Playwright on PRs, upload diffs on failure

**Output/Workflow:**
- First run generates baselines → commit them.
- Later runs compare against baselines → any drift = actionable failure.

---

# 2) Deploy scripts: client to Vercel, API to Render
**What:** Make deployment “one click” for any kit.

**Why:** Quick shareable preview URLs for you or collaborators; verifies that the kit works in a hosted environment (static assets + API CORS).

**What we’d add (per kit):**
- **Client (Vercel)**: minimal `vercel.json` and README snippet telling Vercel to build with `npm run build` in `kits/…/client` and serve `dist/`.
- **API (Render)**: a `render.yaml` or dashboard instructions for Node service at `kits/…/server` (env `PORT=5050`), auto-deploy from your repo.

**Output/Workflow:**
- CI can build and (optionally) deploy on `main` tags or manual promote.

---

# 3) Ingest → Generate flow for a brand-new ZIP
**What:** Use your CLI to bring new templates into the **previewer** (so you can view all variants), then generate a MERN kit from any variant.

**Why:** Scales to your goal of ~10 templates. Keeps previewing and kit generation consistent with the structure you already proved out.

**What you’ll do:**
- `npm run refactor -- ingest --zip <path/to/your.zip> [--slug my-slug] [--variant cyan]`
- Preview it immediately in the left-panel app.
- `npm run refactor -- generate --slug my-slug --variant cyan --out kits/pex-my-slug`
- Run the kit (server & client) and snapshot baselines.

**Output/Workflow:**
- Each template becomes selectable in the previewer.
- Each chosen variant gets its own ready-to-run MERN kit.

---

# 4) Tailwind componentization (real refactor)
**What:** Convert a chosen template’s HTML/CSS/JS into **React components + Tailwind**, clean semantics, and remove jQuery plugins (either replace with small React hooks or modern libs).

**Why:** This is the **value add**—maintainable, modern, accessible code with easy content changes and theming.

**What we’d do (per chosen kit):**
- Break out **Layout** + **Sections** (Hero, Features, Gallery, Footer).
- Create **data files** (e.g., `src/content/home.ts`) so text/images are editable without touching JSX.
- Map legacy CSS vars/tokens into `tailwind.config.js`.
- Replace behaviors (drop menus, smooth scroll, reveal-on-scroll) with tiny React utilities and IntersectionObserver instead of jQuery.
- Keep pixel parity at first, then offer optional “modern tweaks”.

**Output/Workflow:**
- A clean React/Tailwind project, tested by Playwright to guarantee parity.

---

## Recommended order (best-practice flow)

1) **Ingest → Generate** all the templates you plan to evaluate (Point 3).  
   *Reason:* build a stable inventory and confirm every variant renders in the previewer and as a kit.

2) Add **Playwright visual tests** to the kits you care about (Point 1).  
   *Reason:* lock in baselines before refactors; you’ll get instant guardrails.

3) Pick **one** template as your first real refactor and do **Tailwind componentization** (Point 4) on a feature branch.  
   *Reason:* keep scope focused; the tests will keep you honest on visual parity.

4) Wire **deployment** for that kit (Point 2): Vercel (client) + Render (API).  
   *Reason:* now you can share and review externally; later we can template these deploy files to reuse across all kits.

Optional after that:
- Promote the Playwright/CI and deploy scaffolding into the **generator** so every new kit gets them out-of-the-box.
- Add a “content schema” so swapping copy/images is just editing JSON/MD.

---

### My pick for **your next immediate move**
Go with **Step 3 (Ingest → Generate)** for the rest of your templates, then immediately **Step 1 (Playwright)** on the top 1–2 candidates. After that, choose the winner and do **Tailwind componentization** on a branch. Finally, add **Vercel/Render deploy** to that refactored kit.

# What “ingest” does (quick)
- Unzips your template into **`public/template/<slug>/<variant>/...`**.
- Auto-detects variants/pages and **updates** `public/template/manifest.json`.
- You can then see it in the left-panel **previewer** (port **5173**).

---

# Step 0 — switch to a working branch (keep milestone clean)

**Folder:** `~/OneDrive/Documents/template_refactor_gpt/preview-launcher`
```bash
git switch -c feat/ingest-more-templates
```

---

# Step 1 — put your ZIP somewhere reachable

- Place your file under `zips/` (you can create it), e.g.:
  - `zips/px-hyperspace-html.zip`
- If your zip name is different, that’s fine — we’ll set `--slug`.

**Folder:** repo root
```bash
mkdir -p zips
# (Copy your .zip into this folder using Explorer or Finder)
```

---

# Step 2 — run ingest

> Replace the ZIP path and slug to match your file.  
> **Tip:** keep slugs consistent: `px-<template>-html` (e.g., `px-hyperspace-html`).

**Folder:** repo root
```bash
npm run refactor -- ingest --zip ./zips/px-hyperspace-html.zip --slug px-hyperspace-html
```

**What you should see**
- Lines like `✔ Variant cyan → public/template/px-hyperspace-html/cyan`
- `✔ Manifest updated: public/template/manifest.json`

*(If the template has a single style, we’ll auto-create `default/`.)*

---

# Step 3 — start (or reload) the previewer and verify

```bash
npm install    # only if this previewer hasn't been installed on this machine

# expect Local: http://localhost:5173/
```

Open **http://localhost:5173**:
1) Choose your **new template** from the Template dropdown.  
2) Pick a **variant** (e.g., cyan/green/orange or default).  
3) Try pages (index, generic, elements, etc.).

## Troubleshooting (Windows/OneDrive quick fixes)

- **“Deletion failed… try again?”** when switching branches  
  Stop dev servers, then:
  ```bash
  taskkill /F /IM node.exe
  ```
  (Pause OneDrive sync temporarily if it’s locking files.)

- **404s for vendor JS/CSS** in the previewer  
  Look under `public/template/<slug>/<variant>/assets/js` and compare file names to the `<script>` tags in that variant’s `index.html`. If a plugin (e.g., `jquery.scrolly.min.js`) is missing from the original, the previewer will show a 404; that’s expected — it’s a vendor issue in the source. When you later **generate** a kit, our generator **auto-stubs** missing jQuery plugins so the kit won’t crash.

- **Spaces in ZIP path**  
  Quote the path:
  ```bash
  npm run refactor -- ingest --zip "./zips/My Template.zip" --slug px-my-template-html
  ```

TypeError: globby is not a function
    at detectTemplate (C:\Users\boliv\OneDrive\Documents\template_refactor_gpt\preview-launcher\refactor-cli\bin\index.js:52:25)
    at async cmdIngest (C:\Users\boliv\OneDrive\Documents\template_refactor_gpt\preview-launcher\refactor-cli\bin\index.js:98:20)

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ASSISTANT:
Good catch—the error is because recent **globby** is ESM-only. In CommonJS you must import it like:

```js
const { globby } = require("globby");
```

Your CLI currently has:
```js
const globby = require("globby");
```
…so `globby` is an object, not a function → “globby is not a function”.

Here’s the quick fix.

---

## Fix the import, then re-run ingest

**Folder:** `~/OneDrive/Documents/template_refactor_gpt/preview-launcher`

### Option A — one-liner patch (copy-paste)
```bash
node -e "const fs=require('fs');const f='refactor-cli/bin/index.js';fs.writeFileSync(f, fs.readFileSync(f,'utf8').replace(/const globby = require\\(\"globby\"\\);/, \"const { globby } = require('globby');\")); console.log('patched globby import');"
```

### Option B — edit in VS Code
Open `refactor-cli/bin/index.js` and change:
```diff
- const globby = require("globby");
+ const { globby } = require("globby");
```
Save.

---

## Try ingest again

```bash
npm run refactor -- ingest --zip ./zips/px-hyperspace-html.zip --slug px-hyperspace-html
```

**Expected output (examples):**
- `ℹ Extracting ZIP → .tmp/px-hyperspace-html`
- `✔ Variant cyan → public/template/px-hyperspace-html/cyan`
- `✔ Manifest updated: public/template/manifest.json`

Verify the files:
```bash
ls -la public/template/px-hyperspace-html
ls -la public/template/px-hyperspace-html/cyan
```

Open/reload **http://localhost:5173** and select **px-hyperspace-html** in the previewer.

ASSISTANT:
you’re in great shape:

## Quick checks (to prove API is healthy)

**From the browser:**
- `http://localhost:5050/api/health` → should return JSON
- `http://localhost:5174/api/health` → should return the **same** JSON (goes through Vite proxy)

**From terminal (anywhere):**
```bash
curl http://localhost:5050/api/health
curl http://localhost:5174/api/health
```

If both work, you’re done. The 404 you saw was only for `/favicon.ico` at `/`.

---

## Optional: silence the 404 (nice to have)

If you’d like a clean console when you open `http://localhost:5050` directly, add two tiny routes:

**Folder:** `kits/pex-hyperspace-blue/server/src/index.js`  
(Add near the bottom, before `app.listen`.)
```js
// optional niceties to avoid 404 in the browser location bar
app.get("/", (_req, res) => {
  res.json({ ok: true, service: "hyperspace-server", hint: "use /api/health" });
});

// ignore default favicon requests from browsers
app.get("/favicon.ico", (_req, res) => res.status(204).end());
```

Restart the server terminal (Ctrl+C, then):
```bash
npm run dev
```
Now `http://localhost:5050` shows a JSON message and no error.

USER:
before i continue with point 2, explain what is a PR

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

ASSISTANT:
Great question! **PR** stands for **Pull Request** (on GitHub/GitLab/Bitbucket it’s also called a **Merge Request**). It’s a proposal to merge changes from one branch into another—usually from your feature branch into `main`.

## What a PR is (in plain terms)
- A **conversation + review** around a set of commits.
- Lets teammates (or future you) **see the diff**, leave comments, request changes, and approve.
- Can run **checks** (build/tests/linters) before code is allowed to merge.
- Records **why** the change was made (title + description) and becomes part of your project history.

## Typical workflow
1. You work on a branch (e.g., `feat/ingest-more-templates`) and push it to GitHub.
2. Open a PR targeting `main`.
3. Reviewers comment/approve; CI checks pass.
4. Merge the PR (via **Merge**, **Squash**, or **Rebase** strategy).
5. Delete the feature branch (optional).

## Why use PRs (even solo)?
- Forces a clean, reviewable set of changes.
- Keeps `main` stable—only tested, reviewed code lands there.
- Creates a durable changelog with context.

## How to open a PR for your repo
**From GitHub UI**
1. Go to your repo page → you’ll see a banner: *“Compare & pull request”*. Click it.
2. Confirm: **base** = `main`, **compare** = `feat/ingest-more-templates`.
3. Fill in:
   - **Title:** `Ingest Hyperspace template + add MERN kit (blue)`
   - **Description:** What changed, why, how to test, screenshots (your previewer + kit), and any follow-ups (e.g., generate green/purple kits).
4. (Optional) Mark as **Draft** if it’s not ready; convert to ready when done.
5. Click **Create pull request**.

**From the command line (opens a browser)**
```bash
# From repo root with GitHub CLI installed
gh pr create --base main --head feat/ingest-more-templates \
  --title "Ingest Hyperspace template + add MERN kit (blue)" \
  --body "Adds px-hyperspace-html assets (blue/green/purple) to previewer and generates kits/pex-hyperspace-blue. How to test: ... Screenshots: ..."
```

## Merge strategies (which button to pick?)
- **Squash & merge (recommended)**: combines all feature-branch commits into one clean commit on `main`. Great for tidy history.
- **Merge commit**: preserves all commits with a merge commit; useful for large collaborative branches.
- **Rebase & merge**: linear history, but can be trickier; only use if you’re comfortable with rebase.

## What to write in a good PR
- **What & why** (one paragraph).
- **How to test** (exact commands/URLs).
- **Screenshots** (you already have previewer/kit images).
- **Follow-ups** (e.g., “Next: generate green and purple kits, add Playwright baseline”).

That’s it! If you want, I can draft the PR title/body for your current branch so you can paste it into GitHub.

ASSISTANT:
Here’s the quick way to check (and install if needed). I’ll say exactly **where** to run each command.

## Check if GitHub CLI is installed

**Run in (any folder is fine):** `~/OneDrive/Documents/template_refactor_gpt/preview-launcher`
```bash
# Git Bash or CMD
gh --version
```
- If you see a version (e.g., `gh version 2.x.x`), you’re good.  
- If you get “command not found” or “‘gh’ is not recognized…”, it’s not installed.

**Extra checks (optional):**
```bash
# Git Bash
which gh

# PowerShell
where.exe gh
```

## Install GitHub CLI (Windows)

Pick ONE method.

**A) Winget (recommended, built-in on Win10/11)**
**Run in:** any folder
```powershell
winget install --id GitHub.cli -e
```

**B) Chocolatey**
```powershell
choco install gh -y
```

**C) Scoop**
```powershell
scoop install gh
```

(After install, open a **new** terminal so PATH updates.)

## Verify & sign in

**Run in:** `~/OneDrive/Documents/template_refactor_gpt/preview-launcher`
```bash
gh --version          # should print a version now
gh auth login         # guided login (choose GitHub.com → HTTPS → "Login with a web browser")
gh auth status        # should say you're logged in
```

## (Optional) Create the PR from the terminal

**Run in (repo root):** `~/OneDrive/Documents/template_refactor_gpt/preview-launcher`
```bash
gh pr create --base main --head feat/ingest-more-templates \
  --title "Ingest Hyperspace template + add MERN kit (blue)" \
  --body "Adds px-hyperspace-html assets (blue/green/purple) to previewer and generates kits/pex-hyperspace-blue. How to test: npm run dev (5173); kit: server 5050 + client 5174; visit /api/health."
```

If `gh` isn’t found after installing, close and reopen your terminal (or reboot). If you want, tell me which shell you use (Git Bash / PowerShell) and I’ll tailor the exact commands.

## Kill running dev servers (Node/Vite) on Windows

**Find PIDs**
```powershell

netstat -ano | findstr :5050
```

**Kill by PID (replace 1234 with the number you saw)**
```powershell
taskkill /PID 1234 /F
```

Type "TASKKILL /?" for usage.

ASSISTANT:
That error happens because Git Bash rewrites Windows-style switches like `/F` into POSIX-looking paths (e.g., `F:/`). Easiest fixes:

## Use one of these in Git Bash

**Option A (call via `cmd.exe`):**
```bash
cmd.exe /C "taskkill /F /IM node.exe"
```

**Option B (PowerShell inline):**
```bash
powershell -Command "Stop-Process -Name node -Force"
```

**Option C (escape the slashes for Git Bash):**
```bash
taskkill //F //IM node.exe
```

> Any of the three will kill all running Node/Vite dev servers.

### (Optional) Kill only by port
Find PIDs:
```bash
powershell -Command "Get-NetTCPConnection -LocalPort 5173,5174,5050 | Select-Object -Unique OwningProcess"
```
Kill a specific PID:
```bash
powershell -Command "Stop-Process -Id <PID> -Force"
```

After that, continue with your git steps (switch to `main`, etc.).

ASSISTANT:
Great question. Short answer: **Git isn’t “randomly erasing” your kits**—it’s trying to make your working folder match the files that exist on the branch you’re switching to. If a kit folder exists on your current branch but **doesn’t exist on `main`**, Git must **delete it in your working tree** when you checkout `main`. On Windows, the delete often fails because a process (Node/Vite/OneDrive/VS Code) is holding files open, so Git keeps asking.

Here’s how to handle it cleanly, plus options so it stops happening.

---

# Why it happens
- You’re on `feat/ingest-more-templates` which **has** `kits/pex-forty/...`.
- You switch to `main` which **doesn’t** have that kit (yet).
- Git needs to remove those kit files locally to match `main`. That’s expected.
- Windows file locks (Node dev server, OneDrive sync, sometimes VS Code) block deletion → prompt appears.

---

Result: `main` now has the kits → no deletions needed.

### 3) Pick the rollback target

#### If you already have the tag `v0.4.0` (you likely do)

```bash

```

> This puts your **local `main`** exactly at your first PR’s state.

### 4) Push the reset to GitHub (force-update `main`)
```bash

```
> Now the remote `main` also matches your first PR state. (The `--force-with-lease` protects you from clobbering newer remote work unintentionally.)

- If you need something from your stash later:

## Why Git “erased” things earlier
When switching from a branch **that has extra files** (generated kits) to `main` **that doesn’t**, Git must delete those files in your working tree to match `main`. On Windows, any locked files (Node/OneDrive/VS Code) make those deletes fail, which is why we paused/terminated them first.

ASSISTANT:

# MASTER PROMPT — “Template Refactor System (Previewer + CLI + MERN Kits)”

**You are a senior full-stack engineer.** Build a production-ready project that ingests arbitrary HTML template ZIPs, previews variants, and generates runnable MERN+Vite+Tailwind “kits”, with tests and deploy scripts.

## Target environment (strict)
- OS: Windows 10/11 (Git Bash & PowerShell)
- Node: **>= 22** (user currently on 22.x)
- npm: latest
- Editor: VS Code
- Repo root folder name: **`preview-launcher`**
- Package managers: **npm** only

## High-level goals
1) **Previewer app** (Vite+React) at **:5173** that:
   - Reads `public/template/manifest.json`.
   - Lets me pick **Template**, **Variant**, **Page** from dropdowns.
   - Loads the selected static page in an `<iframe>`.
2) **CLI tool** `refactor-cli` with two commands:
   - `ingest`: unzip a template into `public/template/<slug>/<variant>/...` and update `manifest.json`.
   - `generate`: scaffold a **MERN kit** for a chosen template variant into `kits/pex-<name>/`.
   - **Auto-stub** missing jQuery plugins (`jquery.scrolly.min.js`, `jquery.scrollex.min.js`, `jquery.dropotron.min.js`) and **inject a `$` shim** so `$` maps to `window.jQuery`.
3) **MERN kit** per variant:
   - **Server** (Express) at **:5050** with `/api/health` returning `{ ok: true, ... }`.
   - **Client** (Vite+React+Tailwind) at **:5174**:
     - Vite proxy `/api` → `http://localhost:5050`.
     - React Router set up.
     - An `iframe` page that serves `/public/<slug>/<variant>/index.html`.
     - `axios` instance at `/api`.
4) **Playwright visual tests** inside each kit:
   - Run against the **built** client via `vite preview`.
   - Snapshot `index.html` and any of `elements.html`, `generic.html`, `landing.html` if present.
   - Scripts: `test:e2e`, `test:update`.
5) **GitHub Actions CI**:
   - Workflow to install Node, build client, run Playwright tests, and upload screenshot diffs on failure.
6) **Deploy scripts**:
   - **Client → Vercel** (`vercel.json`, build & output configured).
   - **API → Render** (`render.yaml` or README steps).
7) **Docs & hygiene**:
   - Top-level `README.md` and kit-level `README.md`.
   - `.gitignore` excludes `.tmp/`, `zips/`, `kits/*-auto/`.
   - `.gitattributes` enforces `* text=auto eol=lf` (avoid CRLF noise on Windows).

## Critical implementation details
- **Previewer (Vite+React):**
  - Scripts: `"dev": "vite"`, `"build": "vite build"`, `"preview": "vite preview"`.
  - UI: 3 selects (Template, Variant, Page) + an iframe.
  - Data source: `public/template/manifest.json` with shape:
    ```json
    {
      "templates": [
        { "slug": "px-helio-html", "label": "Helio", "variants": ["cyan","green","orange"], "pages": ["index.html","left-sidebar.html","no-sidebar.html","right-sidebar.html"] }
      ]
    }
    ```
  - On change, update the iframe `src` to `/<slug>/<variant>/<page>`.
- **CLI (`refactor-cli/bin/index.js`)**:
  - Language: **CommonJS**.
  - Deps: `fs-extra`, `yargs`, `extract-zip`, `chalk@^4`, `globby`.
  - **Important imports**:
    - `const chalk = require("chalk");` (v4 API uses `chalk.green(...)`).
    - `const { globby } = require("globby");` (**ESM bridge**; don’t use `require("globby")` directly).
  - `ingest`:
    - `--zip <path>` (required), `--slug <string>` (optional), `--variant <string>` (optional).
    - Unzip to `.tmp/<slug>`, detect variants (subfolders or `default`), copy to `public/template/<slug>/<variant>/...`.
    - Update `public/template/manifest.json` with `label` derived from slug (e.g., `px-hyperspace-html` → `Hyperspace`), `variants`, `pages`.
  - `generate`:
    - `--slug <slug>` (required), `--variant <name>` (defaults to `default`), `--out <kits/pex-*>` (required).
    - Create `kits/<out>/{client,server}` structure.
    - **Server**: Express `/api/health`, CORS, morgan, `PORT=5050` via `.env.example`.
    - **Client**: Vite+React+Tailwind; proxy `/api` → `:5050`; React Router; `axios` instance at `/api`.
    - Copy the variant’s static files into `client/public/<slug>/<variant>/...`.
    - **Auto-stub if missing** in `client/public/<slug>/<variant>/assets/js/`:
      ```js
      // jquery.scrolly.min.js
      !function($){$.fn.scrolly=function(){return this}}(window.jQuery||window.$);
      // jquery.scrollex.min.js
      !function($){$.fn.scrollex=function(){return this}}(window.jQuery||window.$);
      // jquery.dropotron.min.js
      !function($){$.fn.dropotron=function(){return this}}(window.jQuery||window.$);
      ```
    - In generated `client/index.html`, **inject after jQuery**:
      ```html
      <script src="/<slug>/<variant>/assets/js/jquery.min.js"></script>
      <script>window.$ = window.$ || window.jQuery;</script>
      ```
      then include the plugins and the template’s `main.js` in correct order.
- **Playwright**:
  - Install `@playwright/test`.
  - `playwright.config.ts`: start `vite preview` server for the kit client, baseURL `http://localhost:5174`.
  - `tests/visual.spec.ts`: visit `/`, take snapshots; if `elements.html`, `generic.html`, `landing.html` exist, also snapshot with timeouts/retries set; provide `npx playwright install --with-deps` in CI.
- **GitHub Actions**:
  - Workflow `.github/workflows/kit-e2e.yml` that:
    - uses `actions/setup-node@v4`,
    - installs deps,
    - builds client,
    - runs Playwright tests,
    - uploads artifacts on failure.
- **Deploy**:
  - **Client**: `vercel.json` with `"buildCommand": "npm run build"`, `"outputDirectory": "dist"`, and project base at `kits/<kit-name>/client`.
  - **API**: `render.yaml` or README that sets `node` service, `buildCommand: "npm i"`, `startCommand: "npm run dev"` or `node src/index.js`, `PORT` env var.

## Output format (strict)
1. **Top-level file tree** (only key files/folders).
2. **Per-file code blocks**, each starting with a comment line of the **relative path**:
   ```
   // path: <relative/path/from/repo/root>
   ```  
   then the file contents in full triple-backticks:
   ```js
   // path: refactor-cli/bin/index.js
   <entire file contents>
   ```
3. **Run-it-now section** with exact commands for Windows (Git Bash/PowerShell), including:
   - Previewer install & start (`npm install`, `npm run dev` → `http://localhost:5173`).
   - Example `ingest` for a ZIP (assume user will place `./zips/<file>.zip`).
   - Example `generate` into `kits/pex-<name>`, then:
     - API: `cp .env.example .env && npm i && npm run dev` → `http://localhost:5050/api/health`.
     - Client: `npm i && npm run dev` → `http://localhost:5174`.
4. **Acceptance checklist** that must pass locally:
   - Previewer runs on **:5173**, dropdowns show the new template and variants.
   - `curl http://localhost:5050/api/health` returns JSON with `ok: true`.
   - `curl http://localhost:5174/api/health` returns same JSON via Vite proxy.
   - No red errors in the browser console (favicon 404 is acceptable).
   - Playwright tests: `npm run test:e2e` pass after baseline is created.
5. **Docs**:
   - `README.md` at repo root describing previewer & CLI usage.
   - `kits/<kit>/README.md` describing how to run API & Client, update snapshots, deploy to Vercel/Render.
6. **Hygiene**:
   - `.gitignore` includes:
     ```
     .tmp/
     zips/
     kits/*-auto/
     node_modules/
     dist/
     ```
   - `.gitattributes` with:
     ```
     * text=auto eol=lf
     ```
   - Use **exact dependency versions** and avoid latest caret where stability matters (e.g., `chalk@^4.1.2`, `extract-zip@^2.0.1`, `fs-extra@^11.2.0`, `yargs@^17.7.2`, `globby@^14.0.2`, Playwright pinned to a stable channel).

## Non-negotiable constraints
- All code must be **copy-paste runnable**; no “pseudo” code.
- Provide **every required file** (no “you know the rest”).
- Use **CommonJS** in the CLI to avoid ESM friction on Node 22.
- Use `const { globby } = require('globby')` (ESM bridge).
- Ensure plugin **load order** in generated clients: `jquery.min.js` → `dropotron` → `scrolly` → `scrollex` → `browser` → `breakpoints` → `util` → `main.js`.
- Include the `$` shim (`window.$ = window.$ || window.jQuery;`) after jQuery.
- Provide robust error messages if a slug/variant path doesn’t exist.
- Keep the React UI minimal, accessible, and resilient.
- Do not prompt the user for more info—**assume sane defaults** and deliver a complete solution.

## Example names to include for smoke testing
- Slugs: `px-helio-html`, `px-forty-html`, `px-elemental-html`, `px-hyperspace-html`.
- Variants: `cyan/green/orange` (for Helio/Elemental/Forty), and `blue/green/purple` (for Hyperspace). If a template has only one style, treat as `default`.

## How to bundle into a ZIP

**Step 1 — Download the three Markdown files** (from the canvas):
- `MASTER_PROMPT_Template_Refactor_System.md`
- `MASTER_PROMPT_LITE_Template_Refactor_System.md`
- `TemplateRefactorPrompts_README.md`

Save them to a single folder, e.g. `C:\Users\boliv\Downloads\template-refactor-prompts`.

**Step 2 — Create the ZIP (pick one):**

### PowerShell (Windows)
**Folder:** `C:\Users\boliv\Downloads\template-refactor-prompts`
```powershell
cd $HOME\Downloads\template-refactor-prompts
Compress-Archive -Path @(
  'MASTER_PROMPT_Template_Refactor_System.md',
  'MASTER_PROMPT_LITE_Template_Refactor_System.md',
  'TemplateRefactorPrompts_README.md'
) -DestinationPath 'TemplateRefactorPrompts.zip' -Force
```

### Git Bash
**Folder:** `~/Downloads/template-refactor-prompts`
```bash
cd ~/Downloads/template-refactor-prompts
zip -r TemplateRefactorPrompts.zip \
  MASTER_PROMPT_Template_Refactor_System.md \
  MASTER_PROMPT_LITE_Template_Refactor_System.md \
  TemplateRefactorPrompts_README.md
```

That’s it—now you’ve got **TemplateRefactorPrompts.zip** ready to share with any LLM. Want me to also generate a tiny “sanity test” prompt (like 5 lines) to quickly check an LLM’s ability before using the full prompt?

## Fix the checkout prompt step-by-step

**Folder:** `~/OneDrive/Documents/template_refactor_gpt/preview-launcher`
```bash
# 1) Save anything (you already stashed, fine to do again)
git stash push -u -m "WIP before forced switch to main"

# 2) Stop common lockers
powershell -Command "Stop-Process -Name node -Force" || true
powershell -Command "Stop-Process -Name Code -Force" || true
# also pause OneDrive from the tray icon (Pause syncing → 2 hours)

# 3) Clear read-only and remove the blocking dir
# PowerShell (recommended)
attrib -R -S -H /S /D "forty-mern\.github\workflows"
rmdir /S /Q "forty-mern\.github\workflows"

# If you prefer Git Bash instead of PowerShell:
# chmod -R u+w "forty-mern/.github/workflows" 2>/dev/null || true
# rm -rf "forty-mern/.github/workflows"

# 4) Clean tree and switch
git reset --hard
git checkout -f main
git pull --ff-only

# 5) Verify
git branch --show-current     # should print: main
git status --porcelain        # should be empty
```

If any path still refuses deletion, paste the exact path it prints and I’ll give you a one-liner for that folder.
